It's a lot lot more complicated than what it seems like.

  <div data-name="Nicole McDonald" data-vid="WFR3lOm_xhE" data-cid="z124jtx51pugujb4g04chtirvoy5zzhivsc0k.1418253778457487" data-aid="100420067789749641549" class="comment-item yt-commentbox-top reply">

        <div class="comment-text">
<div class="comment-text-content">Well... To a certain extent, he can.

For example, if you were to ask him "List all of the universities in Glasgow" he'd be able to produce a list.
But if you asked him instead "List all of the universities in Scotland's biggest city," he learns to make certain associations. 

If you said something about the US President in a question, Watson would analyse and discover the meaning of the abbreviation "US," then discover the meaning of the word "President" - and learn through experience that, more often than not, these two words are used in proximity to each other, therefore associating them.

He's improving, at least.</div>    <div class="comment-text-toggle hid">

  <div data-name="Erik Vega" data-vid="WFR3lOm_xhE" data-cid="z13ncxnztuejx3lku223cjqhykypevh4f04.1409723540659839" data-aid="113518779573421619291" class="comment-item yt-commentbox-top reply">


    <a data-ytid="113518779573421619291" class="g-hovercard" target="_blank" href="/channel/UCus4P41cW01Z8cESqXZnU5g">
      <img width="32" src="https://yt3.ggpht.com/-58HmILY9i9c/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAAA/3U6cdFecrZI/s32-c-k-no/photo.jpg" class="user-photo" />
    </a>
    <div class="content">
        <div class="comment-header">
    <a data-ytid="113518779573421619291" target="_blank" class="user-name g-hovercard" href="/channel/UCus4P41cW01Z8cESqXZnU5g">Erik Vega</a>
    <span class="spacer"></span>
    <span class="time">
        <a target="_blank" href="/watch?v=WFR3lOm_xhE&amp;lc=z13ncxnztuejx3lku223cjqhykypevh4f04">
          1 year ago
        </a>
    </span>
  </div>

        <div class="comment-text">
<div class="comment-text-content">Also, the act of answering the question is more complex then it sounds. Think about it. When you read what I say you have to be able to recognize what different sounds are being used together, then dicpher what their meaning is and turn that into some type of code to search for some phrase and answer in a database and then turn that into a coherent answer and response and then be able to use that answer in the future to answer a similar answer again based on information learned. The simple fact is that besides humans, no other creature we know of can do that on such a complex level. The closest is dolphins, then sorta: dogs, cats, elephants and whales. But they can't understand our complex language and all the rules and behaviors that have been created into it over thousands of years and ideas. The fact is, if a computer is able to outbeat us, it's a matter of time before a computer is able to outthink us. 

Want to talk about being able to sustain the technological growth? Or travel to the ends of the universe? Have a computer solve the problem for you. Have it create the technology. Then create the technology that should come after that. And then the ones after that. Realistically we're limited in intelligence, but if we can use something that is only meant to solve problems in our universe we have, then we'd be able to grow in such an amazing unprecedented way. 

The fact is, it's a big big deal. </div>    <div class="comment-text-toggle hid">

        <div class="comment-text">
<div class="comment-text-content">I'm sorry <a data-sessionlink="ei=1PUuVoSpC4KbuQK99J7oCg" class="yt-uix-sessionlink      " href="/user/yuli2192">+yuli2192</a> but I think you don't have enough knowledge to judge this as being dumb or retarded.
To a computer program, a database is like a person's memory. Its not cheating. The computer stores his knowledge in the database and the person stores knowledge in his memory. The thing is that humans forget things but the database does not.

The relevant thing is that the computer is understanding the question, and knows what record of his database constitutes the answer. This, is not trivial, dumb nor retarded. It is a very complex problem for computers to solve.

I agree with you though that watson did not destroyed anyone as the other participants did a fairly good job.</div>    <div class="comment-text-toggle hid">
